interface LanguageProviderProps {
  children: ReactNode;
}
 
export const LanguageProvider: React.FC<LanguageProviderProps> = ({ children }) => {
  const [language, setLanguageState] = useState<Language>('en'); // Varsaylan ngilizce
  const [currency, setCurrency] = useState<Currency>('USD'); // Varsaylan USD
 
  // Dil ve para birimi ayarn ykle
  useEffect(() => {
    loadLanguageAndCurrency();
  }, []);
 
  const loadLanguageAndCurrency = async () => {
    try {
      // Kaydedilmi dili ykle
      const detectedLanguage = await detectLanguage();
      const detectedCurrency = detectCurrency(detectedLanguage);
      
      logger.log('Yklenen dil:', detectedLanguage);
      logger.log('Yklenen para birimi:', detectedCurrency);
      
      setLanguageState(detectedLanguage);
      setCurrency(detectedCurrency);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Dil ve para birimi ykleme hatas:', error);
      setLanguageState('en'); // Hata durumunda ngilizce
      setCurrency('USD'); // Hata durumunda USD
    }
  };
 
  const setLanguage = async (lang: Language) => {
    try {
      // Kullanc dil seimine izin ver
      setLanguageState(lang);
      await AsyncStorage.setItem('appLanguage', lang);
      
      // Dil deitiinde para birimini de gncelle
      const newCurrency = detectCurrency(lang);
      setCurrency(newCurrency);
      logger.log('Dil deiiklii kaydedildi:', lang);
      logger.log('Para birimi gncellendi:', newCurrency);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Dil kaydetme hatas:', error);
    }
  };
 
  const t = (key: string): string => {
    return translations[language][key] || key;
  };
 
  return (
    <LanguageContext.Provider value={{ language, setLanguage, t, currency }}>
      {children}
    </LanguageContext.Provider>
  );
};
 
export const useLanguage = (): LanguageContextType => {
  const context = useContext(LanguageContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('useLanguage must be used within a LanguageProvider');
  }
  return context;
};
